Q: What -- what is a oulk tote exactly?

It's more efficient for the pharmacy - they get a lot of product at once in one container rather than having to handle dozens of individual shipments. Good for inventory management and cost savings.

For a high-volume product like hydrocodone, offering bulk totes made sense because pharmacies were going through a lot of it and wanted the convenience of bulk packaging.

Pretty standard packaging option in the generics business.

A: Well, pedigree laws are generally about preventing counterfeit drugs and maintaining the integrity of the pharmaceutical supply chain.
